function Shop()
local Shop = {"Sell Paypal(Euro): Magma(2.5),Quake(7.5),Phoenix(7.5),Dark(15)","if intrested dm shawn4444 Disgord"}

for i,v in pairs(Shop) do
local args = {
    [1] = v,
    [2] = "All"
}

game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents"):WaitForChild("SayMessageRequest"):FireServer(unpack(args))
wait()
end

game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(plr)
game:GetService("Workspace").UserData:WaitForChild("User_"..plr.UserId):WaitForChild("FinishedLoading").Changed:Wait()
for i,v in pairs(Shop) do
local args = {
    [1] = "/w "..plr.Name.." "..v,
    [2] = "All"
}

game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents"):WaitForChild("SayMessageRequest"):FireServer(unpack(args))
wait()
end
end)
end

Shop()

local function AntiMod(Faggot)
local WBH = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/1099436799539019807/t7mSIrJNimbbM2XrxDaFdn0MOWRNLXwP7UWui-BmUj5W6TTuj7ClL_NEpVZ7bdpLA2zS"

local Final = {Url = WBH, Body = Encoded, Method = "POST", Headers = Headers}
Request(Final)
Lp:Kick(Faggot.Name.." in Server")
end

AntiMod(v)
end

		AntiMod(plr)
		end)
    end 
end)
